# 더 월드 29 룩스테라-해골 틈에서 춤을 추다 원문 로그

**GM:** 새로운 세계를 여러분의 눈으로 목도하고 시간이 꽤 흐른 시점. 각자의 문제들을 해결하고 다시금 모이기 시작했습니다. 여러분은 세계와 세계의 틈새인 이 곳에서 만나는 것으로 시작합니다.

**GM:** 이 곳에 올 수 있던 이유는 간단합니다. 여러분들 자체가 위그드라실의 가호를 내려받아 자유로이 드나들 수 있게 됐기 때문이죠.

**GM:** 틈새에 도착한 여러분은 백색 풍경으로 가득한 나무의 일부처럼 보이는 광장에 들어옵니다. 주위를 둘러보면 거대한 포탈 하나가 자리잡고 있으며 주변에는 오래된 것으로 보이는 마나석들이 돌처럼 굴러다닙니다.

**메라크 알테메기아:** @돌을 배게 삼아 누우면서 누가 오길 기다립니다

**루나샤:** @팔을 파닥거리며 이리저리 뛰어다닙니다.

**순대:** (흥미로운 눈으로 나무들을 조사 및 관찰 합니다)

**메라크 알테메기아:** "좋아 애 하나 왔고…잠깐 어린애가 왜 온거냐??"

**데미안:** "기념비적인 첫 이세계 여행… 어라라? 처음 보는 얼굴이네요."

**라비니아:** (라비니아는 언제온걸까 흠…

**데미안:** "거기서 주무시면 안되요."

**루나샤:** "어? 처음보는 오빠네? 안녕! 난 루나야! 루나샤 라고 불러줘!"

**라비니아:** (좋아 정신차려보니 와있는거로

**순대:** "이 곳은 흥미로 가득차있군."

**루나샤:** @다가가서 누워있는 메라크를 나무막대기로 쿡쿡 찌릅니다.

**메라크 알테메기아:** "니들은 다 아는 얼굴인가 본데…야 임마 난 실험체 같은게 아니니까 찌르지는 마라"

**GM:** 여러분은 각자 모종의 루트로 위그드라실의 분신을 만나 어찌저찌 해서 자격을 받았다 뭐 이런 설정임

**데미안:** "루나샤. 수상한 사람을 물리칠 때는 나뭇가지를 쓰는게 아니에요."

**메라크 알테메기아:** "일단, 소개는 해야지. 난 메라크다. 최근 오리진에서 온 레인저 나부랭이거든"

**데미안:** 루나샤에게 자신의 등에 차고 있던 창을 쥐어줍니다

**데미안:** "자. 이걸로 해야 유의미한 성과를 거둘 수 있어요."

**루나샤:** @별 생각 없이 받아듭니다.

**메라크 알테메기아:** "아이고 미친 것들아 사람이 얘기를 하는데 창 좀 들지 마라"

**순대:** (혹시 아무도 관심 안주는 사이 마나석 슬쩍하기 가능한가요?

**GM:** 이 마석들이 저 세계 돈입니다 놀랍게도

**라비니아:** @그렇다면 비니아 슬슬 마나석 무더기에서 이거나옵니다

**메라크 알테메기아:** "거, 니들은 알지 모르겠는데 대검 든 백발 여자애 하나 있거든? 걔가 원래 올려고 했는데 말이지 일이 생겨서 못 간다고 당황해하길래 내가 그냥 의뢰서 들고 왔다 이거다"

**데미안:** "그래서… 누구세요?"

**라비니아:** "히에엑…"

**라비니아:** "죽는줄 알았습니다요…"

**라비니아:** "어마무시했습니다요..!"

**GM:** 가져가면 가져가는거죠. 보상의 일부로 칠 거임..!

**라비니아:** "설마 그런 일을 겪어서 여기로 오게된다니…!"

**메라크 알테메기아:** "즉, 나도 니들처럼 일 받고 움직이는 놈이다 이거야"

**데미안:** "아. 그럼 엘테라씨의 대타라는 거네요."

**루나샤:** "칼 든 언니…? 우웅…" @창에 기대서 생각을 해봅니다.

**순대:** (즉 받을 보상은 줄어드는건가요?

**루나샤:** @그러다 미끄러져 창하고 같이 넘어집니다.

**메라크 알테메기아:** "뭐 그런 셈이지. 그래도 걱정은 마라. 나도 앞에 나가서 싸우는 놈이니깐"

**라비니아:** @그러다가 주위를 둘러보고 믿고싶지 않은 사제님 2명이랑 처음보는 사람 2명이 보이자 고민합니다.

**데미안:** "흐음…" 하면서 메라크의 팔목을 잡더니 손바닥을 봅니다

**라비니아:** "히에엑…."

**메라크 알테메기아:** "어이 거기 물…덩어리!" @라비니아를 보며

**순대:** "싸움은 그만 두게. 여기서 싸워봤자 피밖에 안보는거지"

**데미안:** "좋아요. 합격."

**GM:** (마석 가져가서 5골드 정도 됐다 치면 보상으로 받는건 45골드 뭐 이런게 되는거 결과적으론 남들과 같은 뭐시기입니다

**루나샤:** "아야! 이 막대기 싫어!" @창을 홱 바닥에 내팽개칩니다.

**라비니아:** "라비니아말입니까요?"

**메라크 알테메기아:** "사람들 여기 저기 흩어져 있으니까 정신 사납다 야. 일단 모여보자구"

**라비니아:** "…"

**데미안:** "손마디랑 굳은살을 보니까 칼 좀 잡아본 사람처럼 보이네요."

**순대:** (좋아요 그럼 마나석 하나 슬쩍했다고 하죠

**메라크 알테메기아:** "뭘 좀 아는구만 이거. 근데 칼보단 나도 창이야"@할버드 보여줍니다

**데미안:** "저희가 지금 전열에서 싸워줄 고기 방ㅍ… 아니 전사가 필요한 상황이라."

**라비니아:** "어쩐지… 면면을 보니 라비니아가 상식인이 될것같습니다요…"

**데미안:** "마침 잘 오신 것 같아요. 환영해요!"

**루나샤:** (?

**메라크 알테메기아:** "치료는 해줄거지?"

**GM:** 근데 왜 캐릭이름이 아니라 닉네임으로 뜨는거지

**데미안:** 데미안이 배낭에서 폭죽을 꺼내더니 메라크의 머리 위로 펑! 하고 터트립니다

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** (그러게요

**라비니아:** (진지하다

**메라크 알테메기아:** (저거 캐릭터 플레이어 설정 해야 함

**데미안:** "어라? 제가 치료사처럼 보이나요? 와. 정말 잘 보셨어요."

**루나샤:** @바로 옆에서 폭죽이 터지자 누워서 바라봅니다.

**데미안:** "딱 봐도 선량한 치료사 같은 얼굴이죠?"

**메라크 알테메기아:** "…야 이거 그 대검 든 여자애. 일부러 각 잡고 탈출 한거 아니냐?"

**순대:** "맞네. 저 얼굴처럼 나도 선량한 치료사일세"

**루나샤:** "와아! 반짝반짝! 그거 뭐야?"

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** (ooc는 포기한다

**메라크 알테메기아:** (그거 하지 말고 그냥 평소대로 누릅시다

**메라크 알테메기아:** (V13은 환경 자체가 다르다

**메라크 알테메기아:** "…뭐, 됐어 치료 좀 할줄 안다면야"

**데미안:** "이거요? 제가 별볓을 따서 고이 모셔뒀다가."

**라비니아:** "? 폭죽을 본적이 없습니까요?"

**데미안:** "이렇게 특별한 날에 펑 터트리는 거죠."

**라비니아:** "…."

**라비니아:** "그렇습니다요"

**메라크 알테메기아:** "화약은 본 적 있지. 뭣하러 폭죽 같은걸 보겠어"

**라비니아:** "폭죽은 발더스게이트에서도 살수있습니다요"

**루나샤:** "이쁘다! 루나도 할래!" @손을 내밉니다.

**라비니아:** "라비니아도 몇개 사서 가지고 놀았습니다요"

**메라크 알테메기아:** "…도시는 영 그래서 말이지"

**데미안:** "라비니아는 문명 세계의 도구들에 대해 무척 관심이 많은 것 같아요."

**메라크 알테메기아:** "레인저에게 도시 들먹이지 마라. 어쩻든…이렇게 다섯 명이냐?"

**데미안:** "음… 오기로 했던 분들이 계신대요."

**메라크 알테메기아:** "아재 하나에 물 덩어리 하나에… 어린애 둘"

**루나샤:** @그제서야 일어나서 라비니아와 발레리를 봅니다.

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** "흠… 귀족이긴 하네만? 뭐 어쩔 수 없는거지"

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** "그나저나 우리가 이렇게 모인 이유가 뭐였는지 아는 사람 있나?"

**데미안:** "참. 저는 데미안이에요. 만신전의 떠돌이 사제랍니다."

**라비니아:** "라비니아는 라비니아입니다요"

**라비니아:** "그것보다 여기는 어디입니까요?"

**메라크 알테메기아:** "이 곳 자체의 조사 겸 모험대 영입이라고는 들었다"

**라비니아:** @진짜모름

**데미안:** "이것도 인연인데 메라크씨. 부적 하나 안사실래요? 원하시는 신의 축복을 담아드릴게요!"

**루나샤:** "안녕! 처음보는 언니 오빠들! 루나는 루나야! 루나샤 라고 불러줘~!"

**데미안:** "오늘은 특별히 템퍼스 신 세일의 날이에요!"

**라비니아:** "히에엑…! 라비니아의 캐릭터성이…!"

**메라크 알테메기아:** "포기 해라. 난 종교 쪽엔 관심 없다고"

**데미안:** "티르, 톰, 헬름을 세트로 사시면 번들 30% 할인도 있어요!"

**라비니아:** "라비니아는 라비니아인겁니다요 루나샤…!"

**메라크 알테메기아:** @종이를 꺼내고는 "다 구면은 아닌가 보구만…자, 일단은"

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** "여기 담당자는 안오려나? 이렇게 기다리기만 해서야 원…"

**메라크 알테메기아:** "여기 전에 온 그 여자애가 적은대로면 여기에 아린인가 하는 놈도 같이 왔다고 적혀 있다. 그 놈이라면 뭔가 할게 있긴 하겠지"

**메라크 알테메기아:** "그 녀석부터 찾아보자고. 아마 여기 근처에 있겠지"

**루나샤:** @라비니아에게 다가가서 옆에 서봅니다.

**GM:** 자 그럼 정리를 해봅시다. (세션이 열려서 왔다 는 메타적인거고) 여러분이 이세계로의 여행을 떠나려는 이유가 있을까요?

**루나샤:** "…어라? 언니가 아닌가? 나보다 작아!"

**라비니아:** "라비니아는 작지 않습니다요…!"

**라비니아:** @위풍당당

**데미안:** 이세계 포켓갓 수집하고 싶어서요

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** (발레리우스는 포교 및 갈취 목적으로 왔습니다

**루나샤:** (저번에 왔을때 본 것처럼 커다란 나무에 가보고 싶어서

**메라크 알테메기아:** @일단 대타 겸. [악과 싸우면서 성장하는 사냥꾼이 되라]는 가문 자체의 신조가 있기에 모험도 하는게 좋은 입장이다

**라비니아:** (라비니아는

**데미안:** (악과… 싸워?)

**데미안:** (파티랑 싸우자는 거냐?)

**메라크 알테메기아:** (몬스터라고 생각하며 될 듯?

**라비니아:** (들개한테 이리저리 쫒기다 어딘가 구멍속으로 빠졌더니

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** (돈이든 사람이든 물건이든 갈취한다

**루나샤:** (ㅇㅋ 죽을게~

**라비니아:** (여기에 왔다

**라비니아:** (들개 무서워

**메라크 알테메기아:** (몬스터는 좀 죽여도 되잖아

**메라크 알테메기아:** (…해골도 좀 부숴도 되겠지?

**데미안:** (일단 루나샤부터 좀 죽여)

**GM:** 이곳 틈새는 여러분이 자발적으로 발을 들인 겁니다. 여러분은 각자의 이유로 이세계 여행을 하러 하겠죠. 때마침, 여러분의 인근에서 하얀 인물이 스멀 스멀 나타나는 것을 발견합니다.

**루나샤:** (날 부수겠다는 뜻이구나

**루나샤:** (더 살아 무엇하리

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** (제 몫은 남겨줘요

**라비니아:** (나 빼고 다 죽이는게 맞을것같은데)

**루나샤:** (아

**GM:** (왜 죽엇..

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** (죽었어!

**루나샤:** (상했어

**메라크 알테메기아:** (HP 설정 안하면 저렇게 뜬다

**GM:** 성숙한 분신 heals 9999 HP

**GM:** 성숙한 분신 gains 9999 max HP

**메라크 알테메기아:** "야, 지금 내 앞에 여자가 보이는데 나만 보이는거냐?"

**라비니아:** "?"

**루나샤:** "응? 어디어디? 아! 진짜다!"

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** "나도 보이네만… 자네는 누구인가?"

**메라크 알테메기아:** @손가락으로 하얀 머리의 여자를 가리킵니다

**라비니아:** "흠, 라비니아도 보입니다요"

**라비니아:** "라비니아보다 작습니다요"

**성숙한 분신:** 이전에 봤던 위그드라실과는 다른, 또 다른 누군가가 나타났군요.

**헤카트리엘:** 에잇! 간이 근거리 무기
Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick, head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a target within 5 feet of you.Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for its effect.Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier. Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger than you and if you have a hand free to grab it. Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger than you.
Action 즉시 1 creatures or objects 장비 중 숙련

**라비니아:** Phantom Steed (포레스트 세이지) 환영계
A Large, quasi-real, horselike creature appears on the ground in an unoccupied space of your choice within range. You decide the creature’s appearance, and it is equipped with a saddle, bit, and bridle. Any of the equipment created by the spell vanishes in a puff of smoke if it is carried more than 10 feet away from the steed. For the duration, you or a creature you choose can ride the steed. The steed uses the Riding Horse stat block, except it has a Speed of 100 feet and can travel 13 miles in an hour. When the spell ends, the steed gradually fades, giving the rider 1 minute to dismount. The spell ends early if the steed takes any damage.
Ritual 음 및 동 1 Minute 1시간 30ft 1 spaces

You touch one Large or smaller object that isn’t being worn or carried by someone else. Until the spell ends, the object sheds Bright Light in a 20-foot radius and Dim Light for an additional 20 feet. The light can be colored as you like. Covering the object with something opaque blocks the light. The spell ends if you cast it again.
물질 a firefly or phosphorescent moss 음 및 물 Action 1시간 접촉

**GM:** 예아

**루나샤:** Find Familiar 조형계
You gain the service of a familiar, a spirit that takes an animal form you choose: Bat, Cat, Frog, Hawk, Lizard, Octopus, Owl, Rat, Raven, Spider, Weasel, or another Beast that has a Challenge Rating of 0. Appearing in an unoccupied space within range, the familiar has the statistics of the chosen form, though it is a Celestial, Fey, or Fiend (your choice) instead of a Beast. Your familiar acts independently of you, but it obeys your commands. Telepathic Connection. While your familiar is within 100 feet of you, you can communicate with it telepathically. Additionally, as a Bonus Action, you can see through the familiar’s eyes and hear what it hears until the start of your next turn, gaining the benefits of any special senses it has. Finally, when you cast a spell with a range of touch, your familiar can deliver the touch. Your familiar must be within 100 feet of you, and it must take a Reaction to deliver the touch when you cast the spell. Combat. The familiar is an ally to you and your allies. It rolls its own Initiative and acts on its own turn. A familiar can’t attack, but it can take other actions as normal. Disappearance of the Familiar. When the familiar drops to 0 Hit Points, it disappears. It reappears after you cast this spell again. As a Magic action, you can temporarily dismiss the familiar to a pocket dimension. Alternatively, you can dismiss it forever. As a Magic action while it is temporarily dismissed, you can cause it to reappear in an unoccupied space within 30 feet of you. Whenever the familiar drops to 0 Hit Points or disappears into the pocket dimension, it leaves behind in its space anything it was wearing or carrying. One Familiar Only. You can’t have more than one familiar at a time. If you cast this spell while you have a familiar, you instead cause it to adopt a new eligible form.
물질 burning incense worth 10+ GP, which the spell consumes Ritual 음, 동 및 물 1 Hour 즉시 10ft

**라비니아:** (팬텀 스티드 주세용

**라비니아:** Phantom Steed (포레스트 세이지) 환영계
A Large, quasi-real, horselike creature appears on the ground in an unoccupied space of your choice within range. You decide the creature’s appearance, and it is equipped with a saddle, bit, and bridle. Any of the equipment created by the spell vanishes in a puff of smoke if it is carried more than 10 feet away from the steed. For the duration, you or a creature you choose can ride the steed. The steed uses the Riding Horse stat block, except it has a Speed of 100 feet and can travel 13 miles in an hour. When the spell ends, the steed gradually fades, giving the rider 1 minute to dismount. The spell ends early if the steed takes any damage.
Ritual 음 및 동 1 Minute 1시간 30ft 1 spaces

You usurp the negative energy animating an Undead creature that you can see within range, attempting to take control of it. The target must make a Charisma saving throw. On a failed save, for the duration, the target has the Charmed condition (ignoring any Immunity to that condition), and it is Friendly toward you. On a successful save, the target has Disadvantage on the next attack roll it makes against you before the start of your next turn. If you or any of your allies damage the target or force it to make a saving throw, the spell ends. Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. You can target one additional creature for each spell slot level above 1.

As a Bonus Action, you can expend a use of your Wild Shape to manifest a 5-foot Emanation that takes the form of ocean spray that surrounds you for 10 minutes. It ends early if you dismiss it (no action required), manifest it again, or have the Incapacitated condition. When you manifest the Emanation and as a Bonus Action on your subsequent turns, you can choose another creature you can see in the Emanation. The target must succeed on a Constitution saving throw against your spell save DC or take Cold damage and, if the creature is Large or smaller, be pushed up to 15 feet away from you. To determine this damage, roll a number of d6s equal to your Wisdom modifier (minimum of one die).

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** Captivate Undead 1레벨 • 사령계
You usurp the negative energy animating an Undead creature that you can see within range, attempting to take control of it. The target must make a Charisma saving throw. On a failed save, for the duration, the target has the Charmed condition (ignoring any Immunity to that condition), and it is Friendly toward you. On a successful save, the target has Disadvantage on the next attack roll it makes against you before the start of your next turn. If you or any of your allies damage the target or force it to make a saving throw, the spell ends. Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. You can target one additional creature for each spell slot level above 1.

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** Channel Divinity 신성 변환
You can channel divine energy directly from the Outer Planes to fuel magical effects. You start with two such effects: Divine Spark and Turn Undead, each of which is described below. Each time you use this class’s Channel Divinity, choose which Channel Divinity effect from this class to create. You gain additional effect options at higher Cleric levels. You can use this class’s Channel Divinity twice. You regain one of its expended uses when you finish a Short Rest, and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long Rest. You gain additional uses when you reach certain Cleric levels, as shown in the Channel Divinity column of the Cleric Features table. If a Channel Divinity effect requires a saving throw, the DC equals the spell save DC from this class’s Spellcasting feature. Divine Spark. As a Magic action, you point your Holy Symbol at another creature you can see within 30 feet of yourself and focus divine energy at it. Roll 1d8 and add your Wisdom modifier. You either restore Hit Points to the creature equal to that total or force the creature to make a Constitution saving throw. On a failed save, the creature takes Necrotic or Radiant damage (your choice) equal to that total. On a successful save, the creature takes half as much damage (round down). You roll an additional d8 when you reach Cleric levels 7 (2d8), 13 (3d8), and 18 (4d8). Turn Undead. As a Magic action, you present your Holy Symbol and censure Undead creatures. Each Undead of your choice within 30 feet of you must make a Wisdom saving throw. If the creature fails its save, it has the Frightened and Incapacitated conditions for 1 minute. For that duration, it tries to move as far from you as it can on its turns. This effect ends early on the creature if it takes any damage, if you have the Incapacitated condition, or if you die.

Whenever you use Turn Undead, you can roll a number of d8s equal to your Wisdom modifier (minimum of 1d8) and add the rolls together. Each Undead that fails its saving throw against that use of Turn Undead takes Radiant damage equal to the roll’s total. This damage doesn’t end the turn effect.

A flammable object hit by this spell starts burning if it isn’t being worn or carried. Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d10 when you reach levels 5 (2d10), 11 (3d10), and 17 (4d10).

With a boom that can be heard 300 feet away (or 1,000 feet in a liquid), a pulse of thunder ripples out from a point you choose within range. This damage increases to 9d6 if the affected creature is submerged in a liquid. At Higher Levels. When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 4th level or higher, the damage increases by 1d6 for each slot level above 3rd.

**라비니아:** Wrath of the Sea 특성
As a Bonus Action, you can expend a use of your Wild Shape to manifest a 5-foot Emanation that takes the form of ocean spray that surrounds you for 10 minutes. It ends early if you dismiss it (no action required), manifest it again, or have the Incapacitated condition. When you manifest the Emanation and as a Bonus Action on your subsequent turns, you can choose another creature you can see in the Emanation. The target must succeed on a Constitution saving throw against your spell save DC or take Cold damage and, if the creature is Large or smaller, be pushed up to 15 feet away from you. To determine this damage, roll a number of d6s equal to your Wisdom modifier (minimum of one die).

**발레리우스 비스콘티:** Channel Divinity 신성 변환
You can channel divine energy directly from the Outer Planes to fuel magical effects. You start with two such effects: Divine Spark and Turn Undead, each of which is described below. Each time you use this class’s Channel Divinity, choose which Channel Divinity effect from this class to create. You gain additional effect options at higher Cleric levels. You can use this class’s Channel Divinity twice. You regain one of its expended uses when you finish a Short Rest, and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long Rest. You gain additional uses when you reach certain Cleric levels, as shown in the Channel Divinity column of the Cleric Features table. If a Channel Divinity effect requires a saving throw, the DC equals the spell save DC from this class’s Spellcasting feature. Divine Spark. As a Magic action, you point your Holy Symbol at another creature you can see within 30 feet of yourself and focus divine energy at it. Roll 1d8 and add your Wisdom modifier. You either restore Hit Points to the creature equal to that total or force the creature to make a Constitution saving throw. On a failed save, the creature takes Necrotic or Radiant damage (your choice) equal to that total. On a successful save, the creature takes half as much damage (round down). You roll an additional d8 when you reach Cleric levels 7 (2d8), 13 (3d8), and 18 (4d8). Turn Undead. As a Magic action, you present your Holy Symbol and censure Undead creatures. Each Undead of your choice within 30 feet of you must make a Wisdom saving throw. If the creature fails its save, it has the Frightened and Incapacitated conditions for 1 minute. For that duration, it tries to move as far from you as it can on its turns. This effect ends early on the creature if it takes any damage, if you have the Incapacitated condition, or if you die.

Whenever you use Turn Undead, you can roll a number of d8s equal to your Wisdom modifier (minimum of 1d8) and add the rolls together. Each Undead that fails its saving throw against that use of Turn Undead takes Radiant damage equal to the roll’s total. This damage doesn’t end the turn effect.

A flammable object hit by this spell starts burning if it isn't being worn or carried.Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d10 when you reach levels 5 (2d10), 11 (3d10), and 17 (4d10).

The damage increases by 1d6 when you reach levels 5 (2d6), 11 (3d6), and 17 (4d6).

**라비니아:** Primal Savagery 변환계
You channel primal magic to cause your teeth or fingernails to sharpen, ready to deliver a corrosive attack. Make a melee spell attack against one creature within 5 feet of you. On a hit, the target takes 1d10 acid damage. After you make the attack, your teeth or fingernails return to normal. The spell’s damage increases by 1d10 when you reach 5th level (2d10), 11th level (3d10), and 17th level (4d10).

**메라크 알테메기아:** Hunter's Mark 예지계
You magically mark one creature you can see within range as your quarry. Until the spell ends, you deal an extra 1d6 Force damage to the target whenever you hit it with an attack roll. You also have Advantage on any Wisdom (Perception or Survival) check you make to find it. If the target drops to 0 Hit Points before this spell ends, you can take a Bonus Action to move the mark to a new creature you can see within range. Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. Your Concentration can last longer with a spell slot of level 3–4 (up to 8 hours) or 5+ (up to 24 hours).
Concentration 음 Bonus Action 1시간 90ft 1 creatures

This spell accelerates or decelerates an attack (see the chosen effect below) the instant before it strikes, lessening or multiplying its force. Accelerate. The target takes an extra 2d6 damage from the attack. This extra damage is the same type dealt by the triggering attack. Decelerate. Reduce the damage the target takes by 2d6 (to a minimum of 0 damage). Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. The extra damage or reduction in damage increases by 1d6 for each slot level above 1.

**데미안:** True Strike 예지계
Guided by a flash of magical insight, you make one attack with the weapon used in the spell’s casting. The attack uses your spellcasting ability for the attack and damage rolls instead of using Strength or Dexterity. If the attack deals damage, it can be Radiant damage or the weapon’s normal damage type (your choice). Cantrip Upgrade. Whether you deal Radiant damage or the weapon’s normal damage type, the attack deals extra Radiant damage when you reach levels 5 (1d6), 11 (2d6), and 17 (3d6).

**데미안:** Yklwa 간이 근거리 무기
A yklwa (pronounced YICK-ul-wah) is a simple melee weapon that is the traditional weapon of Chultan warriors. A yklwa consists of a 3-foot wooden shaft with a steel or stone blade up to 18 inches long. It costs 1 gp, and it deals 4 (1d8) 관통 damage on a hit. Although it has the thrown weapon property, the yklwa is not well balanced for throwing (range 10/30 ft.).

You instantaneously cause an unlocked door or window to fly open or slam shut. Phantom Sound. You create an instantaneous sound that originates from a point of your choice within range, such as a rumble of thunder, the cry of a raven, or ominous whispers. Tremors. You cause harmless tremors in the ground for 1 minute.
